[step 7] -> Write "{\"path\": \"src/llm/openai.rs\", \"contents\": \"//! OpenAI-compatible chat-completions adapter.\\n//!\\n//! Targets the `/chat/completions` shape that OpenAI, Azure (via gateway),\\n//! GLM (Zhipu), DeepSeek, Moonshot, Together, Ollama and many others speak.\\n//! The only thing that varies is the base URL + model name + API key, which\\n//! is all driven by config.\\n//!\\n//! ## Deferred tool loading\\n//!\\n//! This provider supports deferred tool loading via a search loop (similar to\\n//! the Anthropic provider). On the first call, only eager tools are sent to the\\n//! model along with a synthetic `ToolSearchTool`. When the model calls\\n//! `ToolSearchTool`, the deferred tool schemas are resolved and injected into\\n//! the next request as a `tool_result` message. The model can then call the\\n//! resolved deferred tools in subsequent rounds.\\n//!\\n//! The search loop is bounded by `MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS` (default 3) to prevent\\n//! infinite loops.\\n\\nuse std::sync::Arc;\\n\\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\\nuse reqwest::Client;\\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\\nuse serde_json::Value;\\nuse std::time::Duration;\\n\\nuse super::search::{KeywordSearchEngine, SpecWithHint, ToolSearchEngine};\\nuse super::StructuredRequest;\\nuse super::{Completion, LlmProvider, RetryPolicy, StreamSender, TokenUsage, ToolCall, ToolSpec};\\nuse crate::error::{Error, Result};\\nuse crate::message::{Message, Role};\\n\\n/// The name of the `ToolSearchTool` we register as a regular tool\\n/// in the eager list. The model calls it like any other function\\n/// tool; we recognize it by name and short-circuit the response\\n/// with a `tool_result` containing the resolved tool schemas.\\npub(crate) const TOOL_SEARCH_TOOL_NAME: &str = \\\"ToolSearchTool\\\";\\n\\n/// Hard cap on the number of search round-trips per\\n/// `complete_with_search` call. Bounds the worst case where the\\n/// model keeps calling `ToolSearchTool` with different queries.\\nconst MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS: usize = 3;\\n\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\\npub struct OpenAiProvider {\\n    base_url: String,\\n    api_key: String,\\n    model: String,\\n    client: Client,\\n    temperature: f64,\\n    max_tokens: u32,\\n    retry: RetryPolicy,\\n    stream_tx: Option<StreamSender>,\\n    /// Algorithm used to resolve a `ToolSearchTool` query into a\\n    /// list of deferred tool names. Always non-null (defaults to\\n    /// `KeywordSearchEngine`).\\n    search_engine: Arc<dyn ToolSearchEngine>,\\n}\\n\\nimpl OpenAiProvider {\\n    pub fn new(\\n        base_url: impl Into<String>,\\n        api_key: impl Into<String>,\\n        model: impl Into<String>,\\n    ) -> Self {\\n        Self {\\n            base_url: base_url.into().trim_end_matches('/').to_string(),\\n            api_key: api_key.into(),\\n            model: model.into(),\\n            client: Client::builder()\\n                .timeout(Duration::from_secs(180))\\n                .build()\\n                .expect(\\\"reqwest client build\\\"),\\n            temperature: 0.2,\\n            // DeepSeek defaults to a per-response cap of 4096 tokens; any\\n            // tool call whose `arguments` string holds more than that — e.g.\\n            // a `write_file` with a multi-kilobyte `contents` field — gets\\n            // truncated server-side and arrives as malformed JSON. 16384 is\\n            // both within DeepSeek's hard ceiling (8192 for v3, 32K-64K for\\n            // newer models) and big enough for whole-file writes. Callers\\n            // can override with `with_max_tokens` if their provider supports\\n            // more or needs less.\\n            max_tokens: 16384,\\n            retry: RetryPolicy::default(),\\n            stream_tx: None,\\n            search_engine: Arc::new(KeywordSearchEngine::new()),\\n        }\\n    }\\n\\n    /// Enable streaming by providing a channel sender for partial tokens.\\n    pub fn with_stream_tx(mut self, tx: StreamSender) -> Self {\\n        self.stream_tx = Some(tx);\\n        self\\n    }\\n\\n    /// Build an `Error::Llm` with the model name prefixed.\\n    fn make_err(&self, ctx: impl Into<String>) -> Error {\\n        Error::Llm {\\n            provider: self.model.clone(),\\n            message: ctx.into(),\\n        }\\n    }\\n\\n    pub fn with_temperature(mut self, t: f64) -> Self {\\n        self.temperature = t;\\n        self\\n    }\\n\\n    pub fn with_max_tokens(mut self, n: u32) -> Self {\\n        self.max_tokens = n;\\n        self\\n    }\\n\\n    pub fn with_retry_policy(mut self, policy: RetryPolicy) -> Self {\\n        self.retry = policy;\\n        self\\n    }\\n\\n    /// Replace the default `KeywordSearchEngine` with a custom\\n    /// implementation. Useful for tests that want to assert on\\n    /// which tools the search returns.\\n    pub fn with_search_engine(mut self, engine: Arc<dyn ToolSearchEngine>) -> Self {\\n        self.search_engine = engine;\\n        self\\n    }\\n\\n    /// The `ToolSearchTool` spec — registered as a regular tool in\\n    /// the eager list. The model calls it like any other function\\n    /// tool; we recognize the call by `name == \\\"ToolSearchTool\\\"`.\\n    fn tool_search_spec() -> (ToolSpec, Option<String>) {\\n        let description = \\\"Fetches full schema definitions for deferred tools so they can be \\\\\\n            called. Until fetched, only the name is known — there is no parameter schema, so \\\\\\n            the tool cannot be invoked. Use `select:<tool_name>` for direct selection, or \\\\\\n            keywords to search.\\\"\\n            .to_string();\\n        let search_hint = Some(\\\"find search discover discover tools lookup\\\".to_string());\\n        let spec = ToolSpec {\\n            name: TOOL_SEARCH_TOOL_NAME.to_string(),\\n            description,\\n            parameters: serde_json::json!({\\n                \\\"type\\\": \\\"object\\\",\\n                \\\"properties\\\": {\\n                    \\\"query\\\": {\\n                        \\\"type\\\": \\\"string\\\",\\n                        \\\"description\\\": \\\"Query to find deferred tools. Use \\\\\\\"select:<tool_name>\\\\\\\" \\\\\\n                            for direct selection, or keywords to search.\\\"\\n                    },\\n                    \\\"max_results\\\": {\\n                        \\\"type\\\": \\\"integer\\\",\\n                        \\\"description\\\": \\\"Maximum number of results to return (default: 5)\\\",\\n                        \\\"default\\\": 5\\n                    }\\n                },\\n                \\\"required\\\": [\\\"query\\\"]\\n            }),\\n        };\\n        (spec, search_hint)\\n    }\\n\\n    /// The core search-aware loop. Each iteration:\\n    /// 1. Build a request with eager tools (caller's eager +\\n    ///    `ToolSearchTool`) and deferred tools.\\n    /// 2. Send and parse the response.\\n    /// 3. If the model called `ToolSearchTool`, resolve the\\n    ///    query against the deferred candidates, append a\\n    ///    `tool_result` message with the resolved tool schemas,\\n    ///    and recurse.\\n    /// 4. Otherwise return the response.\\n    ///\\n    /// `pending_tool_result` is `Some((tool_use_id, names))` on\\n    /// iterations after the first — it instructs the body builder\\n    /// to include a `tool_result` message that provides the\\n    /// resolved tool schemas to the model.\\n    async fn run_search_loop(\\n        &self,\\n        messages: &[Message],\\n        eager_tools: &[SpecWithHint],\\n        deferred_tools: &[SpecWithHint],\\n        pending_tool_result: Option<(&str, &[String])>,\\n        round: usize,\\n    ) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        // Build the full eager list: caller's eager + ToolSearchTool.\\n        let mut all_eager: Vec<SpecWithHint> = Vec::with_capacity(eager_tools.len() + 1);\\n        all_eager.push(Self::tool_search_spec());\\n        all_eager.extend_from_slice(eager_tools);\\n\\n        let body = build_request_with_partition(\\n            &self.model,\\n            self.temperature,\\n            self.max_tokens,\\n            messages,\\n            &all_eager,\\n            deferred_tools,\\n            pending_tool_result,\\n        );\\n        let url = format!(\\\"{}/chat/completions\\\", self.base_url);\\n        let text = self.post_json_with_retry(&url, &body, \\\"complete_with_search\\\").await?;\\n        let parsed: ChatResponse = serde_json::from_str(&text)\\n            .map_err(|e| self.make_err(format!(\\\"failed to parse response: {e}; body: {text}\\\")))?;\\n        let choice = parsed\\n            .choices\\n            .into_iter()\\n            .next()\\n            .ok_or_else(|| self.make_err(\\\"response had no choices\\\"))?;\\n        let completion = parse_completion(choice, parsed.usage);\\n\\n        // If the model called ToolSearchTool, resolve and recurse.\\n        if let Some(search_call) = completion\\n            .tool_calls\\n            .iter()\\n            .find(|c| c.name == TOOL_SEARCH_TOOL_NAME)\\n        {\\n            if round >= MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS {\\n                tracing::warn!(\\n                    target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                    round,\\n                    max = MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS,\\n                    \\\"ToolSearchTool: hit MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS, returning current completion\\\"\\n                );\\n                return Ok(completion);\\n            }\\n            let query = search_call\\n                .arguments\\n                .get(\\\"query\\\")\\n                .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\\n                .unwrap_or(\\\"\\\");\\n            let max_results = search_call\\n                .arguments\\n                .get(\\\"max_results\\\")\\n                .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\\n                .map(|n| n as usize);\\n            let names = self.search_engine.resolve(query, deferred_tools);\\n            let names: Vec<String> = match max_results {\\n                Some(n) => names.into_iter().take(n).collect(),\\n                None => names,\\n            };\\n\\n            // Build the augmented transcript for the next request:\\n            //   [...prev, assistant_with_call, tool_result]\\n            let mut next_messages: Vec<Message> = messages.to_vec();\\n            let assistant_with_call = Message {\\n                role: Role::Assistant,\\n                content: completion.content.clone(),\\n                tool_calls: completion.tool_calls.clone(),\\n                tool_call_id: None,\\n                reasoning_content: completion.reasoning_content.clone(),\\n            };\\n            next_messages.push(assistant_with_call);\\n            // The tool_result message carries the resolved tool schemas\\n            // as its content (JSON-encoded array of tool specs).\\n            let resolved_content = build_tool_result_content(&names, deferred_tools);\\n            next_messages.push(Message {\\n                role: Role::Tool,\\n                content: resolved_content,\\n                tool_calls: Vec::new(),\\n                tool_call_id: Some(search_call.id.clone()),\\n                reasoning_content: None,\\n            });\\n\\n            return Box::pin(self.run_search_loop(\\n                &next_messages,\\n                eager_tools,\\n                deferred_tools,\\n                Some((&search_call.id, &names)),\\n                round + 1,\\n            ))\\n            .await;\\n        }\\n\\n        Ok(completion)\\n    }\\n\\n    /// Streaming version of the search-aware loop.\\n    ///\\n    /// Each round streams eagerly (with `ToolSearchTool` in the eager list).\\n    /// If the model calls `ToolSearchTool`, we resolve the query, inject\\n    /// the resolved tool schemas, and start a new streaming round. The\\n    /// stream_tx is passed through every round so the user sees tokens as\\n    /// they arrive across all rounds.\\n    async fn run_stream_search_loop(\\n        &self,\\n        messages: &[Message],\\n        eager_tools: &[SpecWithHint],\\n        deferred_tools: &[SpecWithHint],\\n        pending_tool_result: Option<(&str, &[String])>,\\n        round: usize,\\n        stream_tx: Option<StreamSender>,\\n    ) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        // Build the full eager list: caller's eager + ToolSearchTool.\\n        let mut all_eager: Vec<SpecWithHint> = Vec::with_capacity(eager_tools.len() + 1);\\n        all_eager.push(Self::tool_search_spec());\\n        all_eager.extend_from_slice(eager_tools);\\n\\n        let mut body = build_request_with_partition(\\n            &self.model,\\n            self.temperature,\\n            self.max_tokens,\\n            messages,\\n            &all_eager,\\n            deferred_tools,\\n            pending_tool_result,\\n        );\\n        body[\\\"stream\\\"] = Value::Bool(true);\\n\\n        let completion = self.stream_with_body(body, stream_tx.clone()).await?;\\n\\n        // If the model called ToolSearchTool, resolve and recurse.\\n        if let Some(search_call) = completion\\n            .tool_calls\\n            .iter()\\n            .find(|c| c.name == TOOL_SEARCH_TOOL_NAME)\\n        {\\n            if round >= MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS {\\n                tracing::warn!(\\n                    target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                    round,\\n                    max = MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS,\\n                    \\\"ToolSearchTool (stream): hit MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS, returning current completion\\\"\\n                );\\n                return Ok(completion);\\n            }\\n            let query = search_call\\n                .arguments\\n                .get(\\\"query\\\")\\n                .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\\n                .unwrap_or(\\\"\\\");\\n            let max_results = search_call\\n                .arguments\\n                .get(\\\"max_results\\\")\\n                .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\\n                .map(|n| n as usize);\\n            let names = self.search_engine.resolve(query, deferred_tools);\\n            let names: Vec<String> = match max_results {\\n                Some(n) => names.into_iter().take(n).collect(),\\n                None => names,\\n            };\\n\\n            let mut next_messages: Vec<Message> = messages.to_vec();\\n            let assistant_with_call = Message {\\n                role: Role::Assistant,\\n                content: completion.content.clone(),\\n                tool_calls: completion.tool_calls.clone(),\\n                tool_call_id: None,\\n                reasoning_content: completion.reasoning_content.clone(),\\n            };\\n            next_messages.push(assistant_with_call);\\n            let resolved_content = build_tool_result_content(&names, deferred_tools);\\n            next_messages.push(Message {\\n                role: Role::Tool,\\n                content: resolved_content,\\n                tool_calls: Vec::new(),\\n                tool_call_id: Some(search_call.id.clone()),\\n                reasoning_content: None,\\n            });\\n\\n            return Box::pin(self.run_stream_search_loop(\\n                &next_messages,\\n                eager_tools,\\n                deferred_tools,\\n                Some((&search_call.id, &names)),\\n                round + 1,\\n                stream_tx,\\n            ))\\n            .await;\\n        }\\n\\n        Ok(completion)\\n    }\\n\\n    /// Send a pre-built request body as a streaming call and return the\\n    /// accumulated `Completion`. Handles HTTP retry internally.\\n    async fn stream_with_body(\\n        &self,\\n        body: Value,\\n        stream_tx: Option<StreamSender>,\\n    ) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        let url = format!(\\\"{}/chat/completions\\\", self.base_url);\\n        let mut attempt = 0;\\n        loop {\\n            tracing::debug!(target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\", request = %body, \\\"POST {url} (stream/search)\\\");\\n            let result = self\\n                .client\\n                .post(&url)\\n                .bearer_auth(&self.api_key)\\n                .json(&body)\\n                .send()\\n                .await;\\n            match result {\\n                Ok(resp) => {\\n                    let status = resp.status();\\n                    if status.is_success() {\\n                        return self.parse_sse_stream(resp, stream_tx.clone()).await;\\n                    }\\n                    let text = resp.text().await?;\\n                    if let Some(backoff) =\\n                        self.retry\\n                            .backoff_for(attempt, Some(status.as_u16()), false)\\n                    {\\n                        tracing::warn!(\\n                            target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                            attempt,\\n                            backoff_ms = backoff.as_millis(),\\n                            status = status.as_u16(),\\n                            \\\"transient HTTP error, retrying (stream/search)\\\"\\n                        );\\n                        tokio::time::sleep(backoff).await;\\n                        attempt += 1;\\n                        continue;\\n                    }\\n                    return Err(self.make_err(format!(\\\"HTTP {status}: {text}\\\")));\\n                }\\n                Err(e) => {\\n                    if let Some(backoff) = self.retry.backoff_for(attempt, None, true) {\\n                        tracing::warn!(\\n                            target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                            attempt,\\n                            backoff_ms = backoff.as_millis(),\\n                            error = %e,\\n                            \\\"network error, retrying (stream/search)\\\"\\n                        );\\n                        tokio::time::sleep(backoff).await;\\n                        attempt += 1;\\n                        continue;\\n                    }\\n                    return Err(self.make_err(format!(\\\"request failed: {e}\\\")));\\n                }\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }\\n\\n    /// POST `body` to `url` with retry, returning the raw response text on success.\\n    ///\\n    /// Handles: network errors, 5xx transient errors, and HTTP 200 with empty body\\n    /// (MiniMax transient failure). All three are retried with exponential back-off\\n    /// according to `self.retry`. Non-transient 4xx errors are returned immediately.\\n    async fn post_json_with_retry(&self, url: &str, body: &Value, label: &str) -> Result<String> {\\n        let mut attempt = 0;\\n        loop {\\n            tracing::debug!(target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\", request = %body, \\\"POST {url} ({label})\\\");\\n            let result = self\\n                .client\\n                .post(url)\\n                .bearer_auth(&self.api_key)\\n                .json(body)\\n                .send()\\n                .await;\\n\\n            match result {\\n                Ok(resp) => {\\n                    let status = resp.status();\\n                    if status.is_success() {\\n                        let text = resp.text().await?;\\n                        if text.trim().is_empty() {\\n                            if let Some(backoff) = self.retry.backoff_for(attempt, None, true) {\\n                                tracing::warn!(\\n                                    target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                                    attempt,\\n                                    backoff_ms = backoff.as_millis(),\\n                                    \\\"HTTP 200 but empty body ({label}), retrying\\\"\\n                                );\\n                                tokio::time::sleep(backoff).await;\\n                                attempt += 1;\\n                                continue;\\n                            }\\n                            return Err(self.make_err(\\\"HTTP 200 but response body is empty\\\"));\\n                        }\\n                        return Ok(text);\\n                    }\\n\\n                    let text = resp.text().await?;\\n                    tracing::debug!(target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\", body = %text, \\\"error response ({label})\\\");\\n\\n                    if let Some(backoff) =\\n                        self.retry\\n                            .backoff_for(attempt, Some(status.as_u16()), false)\\n                    {\\n                        tracing::warn!(\\n                            target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                            attempt,\\n                            backoff_ms = backoff.as_millis(),\\n                            status = status.as_u16(),\\n                            \\\"transient HTTP error, retrying ({label})\\\"\\n                        );\\n                        tokio::time::sleep(backoff).await;\\n                        attempt += 1;\\n                        continue;\\n                    }\\n\\n                    return Err(self.make_err(format!(\\\"HTTP {status}: {text}\\\")));\\n                }\\n                Err(e) => {\\n                    if let Some(backoff) = self.retry.backoff_for(attempt, None, true) {\\n                        tracing::warn!(\\n                            target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                            attempt,\\n                            backoff_ms = backoff.as_millis(),\\n                            error = %e,\\n                            \\\"network error, retrying ({label})\\\"\\n                        );\\n                        tokio::time::sleep(backoff).await;\\n                        attempt += 1;\\n                        continue;\\n                    }\\n                    return Err(self.make_err(format!(\\\"request failed: {e}\\\")));\\n                }\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n#[async_trait]\\nimpl LlmProvider for OpenAiProvider {\\n    #[tracing::instrument(skip(self, messages, tools), fields(\\n        provider = %self.base_url.split('/').next_back().unwrap_or(\\\"unknown\\\"),\\n        model = %self.model\\n    ))]\\n    async fn complete(&self, messages: &[Message], tools: &[ToolSpec]) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        let body = build_request(\\n            &self.model,\\n            self.temperature,\\n            self.max_tokens,\\n            messages,\\n            tools,\\n        );\\n        let url = format!(\\\"{}/chat/completions\\\", self.base_url);\\n        let text = self.post_json_with_retry(&url, &body, \\\"complete\\\").await?;\\n        let parsed: ChatResponse = serde_json::from_str(&text)\\n            .map_err(|e| self.make_err(format!(\\\"failed to parse response: {e}; body: {text}\\\")))?;\\n        let choice = parsed\\n            .choices\\n            .into_iter()\\n            .next()\\n            .ok_or_else(|| self.make_err(\\\"response had no choices\\\"))?;\\n        Ok(parse_completion(choice, parsed.usage))\\n    }\\n\\n    async fn complete_structured(&self, req: StructuredRequest) -> Result<Value> {\\n        let mut body = build_request(\\n            &self.model,\\n            self.temperature,\\n            self.max_tokens,\\n            &req.messages,\\n            &[],\\n        );\\n        body[\\\"response_format\\\"] = serde_json::json!({\\n            \\\"type\\\": \\\"json_schema\\\",\\n            \\\"json_schema\\\": {\\n                \\\"name\\\": req.schema_name,\\n                \\\"strict\\\": true,\\n                \\\"schema\\\": req.schema,\\n            }\\n        });\\n        let url = format!(\\\"{}/chat/completions\\\", self.base_url);\\n        let text = self.post_json_with_retry(&url, &body, \\\"structured\\\").await?;\\n        let parsed: ChatResponse = serde_json::from_str(&text)\\n            .map_err(|e| self.make_err(format!(\\\"failed to parse response: {e}; body: {text}\\\")))?;\\n        let choice = parsed\\n            .choices\\n            .into_iter()\\n            .next()\\n            .ok_or_else(|| self.make_err(\\\"response had no choices\\\"))?;\\n        let completion = parse_completion(choice, parsed.usage);\\n        if completion.content.trim().is_empty() {\\n            return Err(self.make_err(\\\"structured response had empty content\\\"));\\n        }\\n        serde_json::from_str(&completion.content).map_err(|e| {\\n            self.make_err(format!(\\n                \\\"failed to parse structured response as JSON: {e}; content: {}\\\",\\n                completion.content\\n            ))\\n        })\\n    }\\n\\n    async fn stream(\\n        &self,\\n        messages: &[Message],\\n        tools: &[ToolSpec],\\n        stream_tx: Option<StreamSender>,\\n    ) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        // If no stream_tx provided, fall back to the instance-level one\\n        let tx = stream_tx.or_else(|| self.stream_tx.clone());\\n        self.stream_inner(messages, tools, tx).await\\n    }\\n\\n    /// Search-aware completion: model sees eager tools + the\\n    /// `ToolSearchTool`; deferred tools are only sent with their\\n    /// names and descriptions (no parameter schemas) and only become\\n    /// fully callable after the model asks for them via `ToolSearchTool`.\\n    async fn complete_with_search(\\n        &self,\\n        messages: &[Message],\\n        eager_tools: &[(ToolSpec, Option<String>)],\\n        deferred_tools: &[(ToolSpec, Option<String>)],\\n    ) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        self.run_search_loop(messages, eager_tools, deferred_tools, None, 0)\\n            .await\\n    }\\n\\n    /// Search-aware streaming: injects `ToolSearchTool` into the eager list\\n    /// and handles multi-round search across streaming calls.\\n    async fn stream_with_search(\\n        &self,\\n        messages: &[Message],\\n        eager_tools: &[(ToolSpec, Option<String>)],\\n        deferred_tools: &[(ToolSpec, Option<String>)],\\n        stream_tx: Option<StreamSender>,\\n    ) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        self.run_stream_search_loop(messages, eager_tools, deferred_tools, None, 0, stream_tx)\\n            .await\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nimpl OpenAiProvider {\\n    async fn stream_inner(\\n        &self,\\n        messages: &[Message],\\n        tools: &[ToolSpec],\\n        stream_tx: Option<StreamSender>,\\n    ) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        let mut body = build_request(\\n            &self.model,\\n            self.temperature,\\n            self.max_tokens,\\n            messages,\\n            tools,\\n        );\\n        body[\\\"stream\\\"] = Value::Bool(true);\\n        let url = format!(\\\"{}/chat/completions\\\", self.base_url);\\n\\n        // Stream requests need the raw Response object for SSE parsing, so we\\n        // can't use post_json_with_retry (which returns text). Retry only on\\n        // non-2xx and network errors; a successful 2xx hands off to parse_sse_stream.\\n        let mut attempt = 0;\\n        loop {\\n            tracing::debug!(target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\", request = %body, \\\"POST {url} (stream)\\\");\\n            let result = self\\n                .client\\n                .post(&url)\\n                .bearer_auth(&self.api_key)\\n                .json(&body)\\n                .send()\\n                .await;\\n\\n            match result {\\n                Ok(resp) => {\\n                    let status = resp.status();\\n                    if status.is_success() {\\n                        return self.parse_sse_stream(resp, stream_tx.clone()).await;\\n                    }\\n                    let text = resp.text().await?;\\n                    tracing::debug!(target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\", body = %text, \\\"error response (stream)\\\");\\n                    if let Some(backoff) =\\n                        self.retry\\n                            .backoff_for(attempt, Some(status.as_u16()), false)\\n                    {\\n                        tracing::warn!(\\n                            target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                            attempt,\\n                            backoff_ms = backoff.as_millis(),\\n                            status = status.as_u16(),\\n                            \\\"transient HTTP error, retrying (stream)\\\"\\n                        );\\n                        tokio::time::sleep(backoff).await;\\n                        attempt += 1;\\n                        continue;\\n                    }\\n                    return Err(self.make_err(format!(\\\"HTTP {status}: {text}\\\")));\\n                }\\n                Err(e) => {\\n                    if let Some(backoff) = self.retry.backoff_for(attempt, None, true) {\\n                        tracing::warn!(\\n                            target: \\\"recursive::llm\\\",\\n                            attempt,\\n                            backoff_ms = backoff.as_millis(),\\n                            error = %e,\\n                            \\\"network error, retrying (stream)\\\"\\n                        );\\n                        tokio::time::sleep(backoff).await;\\n                        attempt += 1;\\n                        continue;\\n                    }\\n                    return Err(self.make_err(format!(\\\"request failed: {e}\\\")));\\n                }\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }\\n\\n    /// Parse an SSE stream from a successful HTTP response.\\n    ///\\n    /// Reads `data: {...}\\\\n\\\\n` chunks line-by-line, extracts\\n    /// `choices[0].delta.content` deltas, accumulates them, and emits\\n    /// each delta through `stream_tx` if configured. Returns the final\\n    /// `Completion` matching the non-streaming shape.\\n    async fn parse_sse_stream(\\n        &self,\\n        resp: reqwest::Response,\\n        stream_tx: Option<StreamSender>,\\n    ) -> Result<Completion> {\\n        let mut content = String::new();\\n        let mut reasoning_content = String::new();\\n        let mut tool_calls: Vec<StreamToolCall> = Vec::new();\\n        let mut finish_reason: Option<String> = None;\\n        let mut usage: Option<TokenUsage> = None;\\n\\n        // Read the byte stream line by line\\n        let reader = resp.text().await?;\\n        for line in reader.lines() {\\n            if let Some(data) = line.strip_prefix(\\\"data: \\\") {\\n                // Skip the final \\\"[DONE]\\\" marker\\n                if data.trim() == \\\"[DONE]\\\" {\\n                    break;\\n                }\\n\\n                // Parse the JSON chunk\\n                let chunk: Value = serde_json::from_str(data)\\n                    .map_err(|e| self.make_err(format!(\\\"SSE parse error: {e}; data: {data}\\\")))?;\\n\\n                // Extract delta content\\n                if let Some(choices) = chunk.get(\\\"choices\\\").and_then(|c| c.as_array()) {\\n                    if let Some(choice) = choices.first() {\\n                        // Delta content\\n                        if let Some(delta) = choice.get(\\\"delta\\\") {\\n                            if let Some(delta_content) =\\n                                delta.get(\\\"content\\\").and_then(|c| c.as_str())\\n                            {\\n                                if !delta_content.is_empty() {\\n                                    content.push_str(delta_content);\\n                                    if let Some(ref tx) = stream_tx {\\n                                        let _ = tx.send(delta_content.to_string());\\n                                    }\\n                                }\\n                            }\\n                            // Accumulate reasoning_content deltas (DeepSeek thinking mode)\\n                            if let Some(delta_reasoning) =\\n                                delta.get(\\\"reasoning_content\\\").and_then(|c| c.as_str())\\n                            {\\n                                if !delta_reasoning.is_empty() {\\n                                    reasoning_content.push_str(delta_reasoning);\\n                                }\\n                            }\\n                            // Accumulate tool call deltas (OpenAI streaming format)\\n                            if let Some(tool_deltas) =\\n                                delta.get(\\\"tool_calls\\\").and_then(|c| c.as_array())\\n                            {\\n                                for tc_delta in tool_deltas {\\n                                    let index = tc_delta\\n                                        .get(\\\"index\\\")\\n                                        .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\\n                                        .unwrap_or(0) as usize;\\n                                    while tool_calls.len() <= index {\\n                                        tool_calls.push(StreamToolCall::default());\\n                                    }\\n                                    if let Some(id) =\\n                                        tc_delta.get(\\\"id\\\").and_then(|v| v.as_str())\\n                                    {\\n                                        if !id.is_empty() {\\n                                            tool_calls[index].id = id.to_string();\\n                                        }\\n                                    }\\n                                    if let Some(func) = tc_delta.get(\\\"function\\\") {\\n                                        if let Some(name) =\\n                                            func.get(\\\"name\\\").and_then(|v| v.as_str())\\n                                        {\\n                                            if !name.is_empty() {\\n                                                tool_calls[index].name = name.to_string();\\n                                            }\\n                                        }\\n                                        if let Some(args) =\\n                                            func.get(\\\"arguments\\\").and_then(|v| v.as_str())\\n                                        {\\n                                            if !args.is_empty() {\\n                                                tool_calls[index].partial_json.push_str(args);\\n                                            }\\n                                        }\\n                                    }\\n                                }\\n                            }\\n                        }\\n\\n                        // Finish reason (only on the last chunk)\\n                        if let Some(fr) = choice.get(\\\"finish_reason\\\").and_then(|f| f.as_str()) {\\n                            if !fr.is_empty() {\\n                                finish_reason = Some(fr.to_string());\\n                            }\\n                        }\\n                    }\\n                }\\n\\n                // Usage (only on the last chunk for some providers)\\n                if let Some(u) = chunk.get(\\\"usage\\\") {\\n                    let prompt =\\n                        u.get(\\\"prompt_tokens\\\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()).unwrap_or(0) as u32;\\n                    let completion = u\\n                        .get(\\\"completion_tokens\\\")\\n                        .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\\n                        .unwrap_or(0) as u32;\\n                    let total = u.get(\\\"total_tokens\\\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()).unwrap_or(0) as u32;\\n                    let cache_hit = u\\n                        .get(\\\"prompt_cache_hit_tokens\\\")\\n                        .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\\n                        .unwrap_or(0) as u32;\\n                    let cache_miss = u\\n                        .get(\\\"prompt_cache_miss_tokens\\\")\\n                        .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\\n                        .unwrap_or(0) as u32;\\n                    usage = Some(TokenUsage {\\n                        prompt_tokens: prompt,\\n                        completion_tokens: completion,\\n                        total_tokens: total,\\n                        cache_hit_tokens: cache_hit,\\n                        cache_miss_tokens: cache_miss,\\n                    });\\n                }\\n            }\\n        }\\n\\n        // Convert streamed tool calls to final ToolCall objects\\n        let final_tool_calls: Vec<ToolCall> = tool_calls\\n            .into_iter()\\n            .filter(|tc| !tc.id.is_empty())\\n            .map(|tc| {\\n                let args: Value = if tc.partial_json.trim().is_empty() {\\n                    Value::Object(Default::default())\\n                } else {\\n                    serde_json::from_str(&tc.partial_json)\\n                        .unwrap_or_else(|_| Value::String(tc.partial_json.clone()))\\n                };\\n                ToolCall {\\n                    id: tc.id,\\n                    name: tc.name,\\n                    arguments: args,\\n                }\\n            })\\n            .collect();\\n\\n        Ok(Completion {\\n            content,\\n            tool_calls: final_tool_calls,\\n            finish_reason,\\n            usage,\\n            reasoning_content: if reasoning_content.is_empty() {\\n                None\\n            } else {\\n                Some(reasoning_content)\\n            },\\n        })\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n/// Build a request body that splits tools into an eager list and a\\n/// deferred list. Used by the search-aware completion path so the\\n/// model can `ToolSearchTool` the deferred tools' schemas on demand.\\n///\\n/// When `pending_tool_result` is `Some((tool_use_id, names))`, the\\n/// last message in `messages` (which is a tool-result message whose\\n/// `tool_call_id` matches `tool_use_id`) is expected to contain the\\n/// resolved tool schemas as its content.\\nfn build_request_with_partition(\\n    model: &str,\\n    temperature: f64,\\n    max_tokens: u32,\\n    messages: &[Message],\\n    eager_tools: &[SpecWithHint],\\n    deferred_tools: &[SpecWithHint],\\n    pending_tool_result: Option<(&str, &[String])>,\\n) -> Value {\\n    let mut req = serde_json::json!({\\n        \\\"model\\\": model,\\n        \\\"temperature\\\": temperature,\\n        \\\"max_tokens\\\": max_tokens,\\n        \\\"messages\\\": messages.iter().map(serialize_message).collect::<Vec<_>>(),\\n    });\\n\\n    // Build the tools array: eager tools first, then deferred tools.\\n    // For deferred tools, we send only the name and description (no\\n    // parameters) so the model knows they exist but cannot call them\\n    // until the schemas are resolved via ToolSearchTool.\\n    let mut tools_json: Vec<Value> = Vec::with_capacity(eager_tools.len() + deferred_tools.len());\\n    for (spec, _) in eager_tools {\\n        tools_json.push(serde_json::json!({\\n            \\\"type\\\": \\\"function\\\",\\n            \\\"function\\\": {\\n                \\\"name\\\": spec.name,\\n                \\\"description\\\": spec.description,\\n                \\\"parameters\\\": spec.parameters,\\n            }\\n        }));\\n    }\\n    for (spec, _) in deferred_tools {\\n        // Deferred tools are sent with a minimal schema — just the name\\n        // and description, but no parameter schema. The model can see\\n        // them listed but cannot call them until ToolSearchTool resolves\\n        // the full schema.\\n        tools_json.push(serde_json::json!({\\n            \\\"type\\\": \\\"function\\\",\\n            \\\"function\\\": {\\n                \\\"name\\\": spec.name,\\n                \\\"description\\\": spec.description,\\n                \\\"parameters\\\": {\\n                    \\\"type\\\": \\\"object\\\",\\n                    \\\"description\\\": \\\"Schema not yet loaded. Use ToolSearchTool to fetch the full schema.\\\",\\n                    \\\"properties\\\": {},\\n                    \\\"additionalProperties\\\": true,\\n                },\\n            }\\n        }));\\n    }\\n    if !tools_json.is_empty() {\\n        req[\\\"tools\\\"] = Value::Array(tools_json);\\n        req[\\\"tool_choice\\\"] = Value::String(\\\"auto\\\".into());\\n    }\\n\\n    req\\n}\\n\\n/// Build the content string for a tool_result message that provides\\n/// the resolved schemas of the deferred tools the model asked for.\\n///\\n/// The content is a JSON string containing an array of tool specs\\n/// (name, description, parameters) that the model can then call.\\nfn build_tool_result_content(names: &[String], deferred_tools: &[SpecWithHint]) -> String {\\n    let specs: Vec<Value> = deferred_tools\\n        .iter()\\n        .filter(|(spec, _)| names.contains(&spec.name))\\n        .map(|(spec, _)| {\\n            serde_json::json!({\\n                \\\"name\\\": spec.name,\\n                \\\"description\\\": spec.description,\\n                \\\"parameters\\\": spec.parameters,\\n            })\\n        })\\n        .collect();\\n    serde_json::to_string(&specs).unwrap_or_else(|_| \\\"[]\\\".to_string())\\n}\\n\\nfn build_request(\\n    model: &str,\\n    temperature: f64,\\n    max_tokens: u32,\\n    messages: &[Message],\\n    tools: &[ToolSpec],\\n) -> Value {\\n    let mut req = serde_json::json!({\\n        \\\"model\\\": model,\\n        \\\"temperature\\\": temperature,\\n        \\\"max_tokens\\\": max_tokens,\\n        \\\"messages\\\": messages.iter().map(serialize_message).collect::<Vec<_>>(),\\n    });\\n    if !tools.is_empty() {\\n        let tools_json: Vec<Value> = tools\\n            .iter()\\n            .map(|t| {\\n                serde_json::json!({\\n                    \\\"type\\\": \\\"function\\\",\\n                    \\\"function\\\": {\\n                        \\\"name\\\": t.name,\\n                        \\\"description\\\": t.description,\\n                        \\\"parameters\\\": t.parameters,\\n                    }\\n                })\\n            })\\n            .collect();\\n        req[\\\"tools\\\"] = Value::Array(tools_json);\\n        req[\\\"tool_choice\\\"] = Value::String(\\\"auto\\\".into());\\n    }\\n    req\\n}\\n\\nfn serialize_message(m: &Message) -> Value {\\n    let role = match m.role {\\n        Role::System => \\\"system\\\",\\n        Role::User => \\\"user\\\",\\n        Role::Assistant => \\\"assistant\\\",\\n        Role::Tool => \\\"tool\\\",\\n    };\\n    let mut obj = serde_json::Map::new();\\n    obj.insert(\\\"role\\\".into(), Value::String(role.into()));\\n    obj.insert(\\\"content\\\".into(), Value::String(m.content.clone()));\\n    if let Some(id) = &m.tool_call_id {\\n        obj.insert(\\\"tool_call_id\\\".into(), Value::String(id.clone()));\\n    }\\n    // Echo reasoning_content back to the API (required by DeepSeek thinking mode)\\n    if let Some(ref reasoning) = m.reasoning_content {\\n        obj.insert(\\\"reasoning_content\\\".into(), Value::String(reasoning.clone()));\\n    }\\n    if !m.tool_calls.is_empty() {\\n        let calls: Vec<Value> = m\\n            .tool_calls\\n            .iter()\\n            .map(|c| {\\n                serde_json::json!({\\n                    \\\"id\\\": c.id,\\n                    \\\"type\\\": \\\"function\\\",\\n                    \\\"function\\\": {\\n                        \\\"name\\\": c.name,\\n                        \\\"arguments\\\": serde_json::to_string(&c.arguments).unwrap_or_else(|_| \\\"{}\\\".into()),\\n                    }\\n                })\\n            })\\n            .collect();\\n        obj.insert(\\\"tool_calls\\\".into(), Value::Array(calls));\\n    }\\n    Value::Object(obj)\\n}\\n\\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\\nstruct ChatResponse {\\n    choices: Vec<ChatChoice>,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    usage: Option<ResponseUsage>,\\n}\\n\\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\\nstruct ResponseUsage {\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    prompt_tokens: Option<u32>,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    completion_tokens: Option<u32>,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    total_tokens: Option<u32>,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    prompt_cache_hit_tokens: Option<u32>,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    prompt_cache_miss_tokens: Option<u32>,\\n}\\n\\nimpl ResponseUsage {\\n    fn to_token_usage(&self) -> TokenUsage {\\n        TokenUsage {\\n            prompt_tokens: self.prompt_tokens.unwrap_or(0),\\n            completion_tokens: self.completion_tokens.unwrap_or(0),\\n            total_tokens: self.total_tokens.unwrap_or(0),\\n            cache_hit_tokens: self.prompt_cache_hit_tokens.unwrap_or(0),\\n            cache_miss_tokens: self.prompt_cache_miss_tokens.unwrap_or(0),\\n        }\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\\nstruct ChatChoice {\\n    message: ChatChoiceMessage,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    finish_reason: Option<String>,\\n}\\n\\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\\nstruct ChatChoiceMessage {\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    content: Option<String>,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    reasoning_content: Option<String>,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    tool_calls: Vec<RawToolCall>,\\n}\\n\\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize, Serialize)]\\nstruct RawToolCall {\\n    id: String,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    function: RawFunction,\\n}\\n\\n#[derive(Debug, Default, Deserialize, Serialize)]\\nstruct RawFunction {\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    name: String,\\n    #[serde(default)]\\n    arguments: String,\\n}\\n\\n/// Accumulator for tool calls being built from SSE stream events.\\n#[derive(Default)]\\nstruct StreamToolCall {\\n    id: String,\\n    name: String,\\n    partial_json: String,\\n}\\n\\nfn parse_completion(choice: ChatChoice, usage: Option<ResponseUsage>) -> Completion {\\n    let content = choice.message.content.unwrap_or_default();\\n    let reasoning_content = choice.message.reasoning_content;\\n    let tool_calls = choice\\n        .message\\n        .tool_calls\\n        .into_iter()\\n        .map(|c| {\\n            let args: Value = if c.function.arguments.trim().is_empty() {\\n                Value::Object(Default::default())\\n            } else {\\n                serde_json::from_str(&c.function.arguments)\\n                    .unwrap_or_else(|_| Value::String(c.function.arguments.clone()))\\n            };\\n            ToolCall {\\n                id: c.id,\\n                name: c.function.name,\\n                arguments: args,\\n            }\\n        })\\n        .collect();\\n    Completion {\\n        content,\\n        tool_calls,\\n        finish_reason: choice.finish_reason,\\n        usage: usage.map(|u| u.to_token_usage()),\\n        reasoning_content,\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n#[cfg(test)]\\nmod tests {\\n    use super::*;\\n\\n    #[test]\\n    fn parses_plain_text_choice() {\\n        let raw = r#\\\"{\\\"choices\\\":[{\\\"message\\\":{\\\"role\\\":\\\"assistant\\\",\\\"content\\\":\\\"hi\\\"},\\\"finish_reason\\\":\\\"stop\\\"}]}\\\"#;\\n        let parsed: ChatResponse = serde_json::from_str(raw).unwrap();\\n        let c = parse_completion(parsed.choices.into_iter().next().unwrap(), parsed.usage);\\n        assert_eq!(c.content, \\\"hi\\\");\\n        assert!(c.tool_calls.is_empty());\\n        assert_eq!(c.finish_reason.as_deref(), Some(\\\"stop\\\"));\\n        assert!(c.usage.is_none());\\n    }\\n\\n    #[test]\\n    fn \\\"finish_reason\\\":\\\"tool_calls\\\"\\n            }]\\n        }\\\"#;\\n        let parsed: ChatResponse = serde_json::from_str(raw).unwrap();\\n        let c =       assert_eq!(u.cache_miss_tokens, 0);\\n    }\\n\\n    #[test]\\n    fn serialises_assistant_with_tool_calls() {\\n        let msg = Message::assistant_with_tool_calls(\\n            \\\"\\\",\\n            vec![ToolCall {\\n                id: \\\"abc\\\".into(),\\n                name: \\\"Write\\\".into(),\\n                arguments:      .unwrap();\\n        let decoded: Value = serde_json::from_str(args).unwrap();\\n        assert_eq!(decoded[\\\"contents\\\"], \\\"b\\\");\\n    }\\n\\n    #[test]\\n    fn builds_request_without_tools_omits_field() {\\n        let req = build_request(\\\"m\\\", 0.2, 16384, &[Message::user(\\\"hi\\\")], &[]);\\n        assert!(req.get(\\\"tools\\\").is_none());\\n   let req = build_request(\\\"m\\\", 0.2, 1024, &[Message::user(\\\"hi\\\")], &[]);\\n        assert_eq!(req[\\\"max_tokens\\\"], 1024);\\n    }\\n\\n    #[tokio::test]\\n    async fn error_includes_model_name_on_network_failure() {\\n        // Bind a listener on an ephemeral port, then drop it so the port is freed.\\n        // The next connect attempt gets ECONNREFUSED (a network error).\\n        let listener = std::net::TcpListener::bind(\\\"127.0.0.1:0\\\").unwrap();\\n        let addr = listener.local_addr().unwrap();\\n        drop(listener);\\n\\n        // Small sleep so the OS releases the port.\\n        tokio::time::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(20)).await;\\n\\n        let provider = OpenAiProvider::new(format!(\\\"http://{addr}\\\"), \\\"sk-noop\\\", \\\"test-model\\\");\\n        let err = provider\\n            .complete(&[Message::user(\\\"hi\\\")], &[])\\n            .await\\n            .unwrap_err();\\n        let msg = err.to_string();\\n        assert!(\\n            msg.contains(\\\"test-model\\\"),\\n            \\\"error should contain model name: {msg}\\\"\\n        );\\n    }\\n\\n    #[tokio::test]\\n    async fn error_includes_model_name_and_status_on_http_error() {\\n        // Spawn a one-shot TCP listener that sends a 400 response.\\n        let listener = std::net::TcpListener::bind(\\\"127.0.0.1:0\\\").unwrap();\\n        let addr = listener.local_addr().unwrap();\\n\\n        // Use a dedicated thread with a blocking server to avoid tokio issues.\\n        std::thread::spawn(move || {\\n            let (mut stream, _) = listener.accept().unwrap();\\n            use std::io::{Read, Write};\\n            let mut buf = [0u8; 4096];\\n            let _ = stream.read(&mut buf);\\n            write!(\\n                stream,\\n                \\\"HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request\\\\r\\\\nContent-Length: 2\\\\r\\\\nConnection: close\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n{{}}\\\"\\n            )\\n            .unwrap();\\n            stream.flush().unwrap();\\n        });\\n\\n        // Give the server a moment to start\\n        tokio::time::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(50)).await;\\n\\n        let provider = OpenAiProvider::new(format!(\\\"http://{addr}\\\"), \\\"sk-noop\\\", \\\"test-model-http\\\");\\n        let err = provider\\n            .complete(&[Message::user(\\\"hi\\\")], &[])\\n            .await\\n            .unwrap_err();\\n        let msg = err.to_string();\\n        assert!(\\n            msg.contains(\\\"test-model-http\\\"),\\n            \\\"error should contain model name: {msg}\\\"\\n        );\\n        assert!(\\n            msg.contains(\\\"400\\\"),\\n            \\\"error should contain HTTP status: {msg}\\\"\\n        );\\n    }\\n\\n    #[tokio::test]\\n    async fn stream_concatenates_sse_chunks() {\\n        // Spawn a one-shot TCP server that serves a canned SSE response\\n        // with 3 chunks. Assert the returned Completion's content is the\\n        // concatenation of the deltas.\\n        let listener = std::net::TcpListener::bind(\\\"127.0.0.1:0\\\").unwrap();\\n        let addr = listener.local_addr().unwrap();\\n\\n        std::thread::spawn(move || {\\n            let (mut stream, _) = listener.accept().unwrap();\\n            use std::io::{Read, Write};\\n            let mut buf = [0u8; 4096];\\n            let _ = stream.read(&mut buf);\\n            let body = \\\"\\\\\\ndata: {\\\\\\\"choices\\\\\\\":[{\\\\\\\"delta\\\\\\\":{\\\\\\\"content\\\\\\\":\\\\\\\"Hello\\\\\\\"},\\\\\\\"finish_reason\\\\\\\":null}]}\\\\n\\\\n\\\\\\ndata: {\\\\\\\"choices\\\\\\\":[{\\\\\\\"delta\\\\\\\":{\\\\\\\"content\\\\\\\":\\\\\\\" \\\\\\\"},\\\\\\\"finish_reason\\\\\\\":null}]}\\\\n\\\\n\\\\\\ndata: {\\\\\\\"choices\\\\\\\":[{\\\\\\\"delta\\\\\\\":{\\\\\\\"content\\\\\\\":\\\\\\\"World\\\\\\\"},\\\\\\\"finish_reason\\\\\\\":\\\\\\\"stop\\\\\\\"}]}\\\\n\\\\n\\\\\\ndata: [DONE]\\\\n\\\\n\\\";\\n            write!(\\n                stream,\\n                \\\"HTTP/1.1 200 OK\\\\r\\\\nContent-Type: text/event-stream\\\\r\\\\nContent-Length: {}\\\\r\\\\nConnection: close\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n{}\\\",\\n                body.len(),\\n                body,\\n            )\\n            .unwrap();\\n            stream.flush().unwrap();\\n        });\\n\\n        tokio::time::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(50)).await;\\n\\n        let provider =\\n            OpenAiProvider::new(format!(\\\"http://{addr}\\\"), \\\"sk-noop\\\",
